<Review>Wow! What a place! And the staff? Awesome as well!

I had found some feed in an online video and hunted it down. The only problem is that it came from a local supplier in the TX/NM area and so not available to me. Seeing as how I didn't know where else to start I just searched for a local feed store and Douglas Feed came up! So I emailed the site and waited.

<date>1621198259327< /date><Rating>5</Rating><text>Our flight experience with Delta during the pandemic was not that bad but not great.

We checked in at terminal 2, went through TSA in 15 minutes, and headed to the gate.  The gate area was super crowded.  It was a completely full flight.

Here's a tip: if you want to board early and get settled in, check your carry on bag for free at the gate, and they'll let you check it in for free.

We decided to pay for basic economy which got us seats at the very end.  This was fine since it was a short hour flt to Vegas.  They require all to wear a mask with no exceptions.

No snack or drink service available on this short haul flight.  When we landed in Vegas, they deboard by rows.  Not everyone was following this as some lady from row 35 in the back attempted to walk to the front, and then got asked to return to her seat.

<text>With my years of experiments with food, I have realized that chemistry lies at the heart of very exceptional food. As we all know, everything in this universe is made up of atoms that combine to form molecules. Many great chefs are outstanding chemists who have perfected the science behind taste by understanding those molecules. And, when you know the minuscule science behind taste - the perfect combination of the luscious molecules combined, you create an explosion of flavor that remains with you forever. So, I was very excited to delve into molecular gastronomy (with an Indian twist) and try out a restaurant that has been known to specialize in just that - SpiceKlub. This fine-dining joint in Cupertino is a perfect spot for vegetarian food lovers and for others to fall in love with vegetarian food. You may have heard the names of all the food on the menu, but I bet that you have never seen or tasted them like this before.

We started the night off with pav bhaji fondue and pani puri (both pictured). Now to anyone knowledgeable of Indian street food, know what those are. But, in SpiceKlub, it's not that simple. The incredibly creamy and smooth bhaji of the pav bhaji comes in a melting fondue pot with tiny fondue forks that take you back to camping nights by the fire. Hands down, this is the most delicious bhaji I have ever had. The pani puri was innovatively well plated - with the pani in test tubes and the chutneys in syringes - taking us back to our chemistry labs in school.

We went with the Paneer Lazeez (pictured, a must recommendation for all paneer lovers) for the main course. This was another creamy dish that totally melted in our mouths. Went very well with both naan and rice.
We chose the flower pot (pictured) for dessert, which is precisely how it is named - a pot made of chocolate, filled with rasmalai, and topped with powdered pistachio. It also comes with a shovel made of pure chocolate. If you were never a fan of sweet dishes, please order this, and I bet there would be no going back.

Our night only got better with a couple of incredible drinks - the Angry Bird (shhh... it's from their secret drinks menu - go ahead and ask - you won't regret) that comes in the most cutest cocktail glass shaped like a bird (pictured). And then the popular Rowdy (pictured) with bourbon, dehydrated orange wheel, and smoked applewood chips - served in a smoked glass box that genuinely adds to its elegance. We also had the Empress (pictured) with kala khatta and paan with tonic water that constantly bubbled. The drink felt very royal and refreshing - just like a paan at the end of a delicious meal.

To sum up: The ambiance is exquisite, the staff is courteous, the food quality is fantastic and above all the presentation is the crowning glory.</text><response>None</response><Rate>5</Rate><Time>1621554460598<//Time></record></dataset><record>

< review>
We celebrated Valentine's at SpiceKlub as a group of four guests. We'd recommend booking a table in advance since the place is pretty busy. Though the theme of the restaurant is molecular gastronomy, the place is really a new way to experience classic foods. Do not miss ordering the paav bhaaji fondue and the vada paav. We got the moti paneer makhani with roomali roti (which was among the best we've ever had), truffle mushroom biryani was a nice twist to a classic dish. Among cocktails, we cannot recommend the "Empress" enough. The restaurant has good outdoor ambience, friendly staff and acceptably quick service. Plenty of parking too. Overall, a wonderful experience for the money.<//review>

<userid>104996621922847969898<//userid><GmapID>0x808fb5a5aa6d7a0d:0xfa988502d90d8c27</GmapID>< review>
A refreshing hub for bay area vegetarians, long awaited A FINE DINING EXPERIENCE!!!!
Classy ambience, molecular gastronomy and guest oriented service - All under one roof " SPICEKLUB"
Let me first start with our food experience. We were a party of 4 and folks booking the table in advance helps as the place is really busy.
As we were seated by the restaurant manager, our server got us some tear drop shaped Thandai burst as "AMUSE BOUCHE", which was really good, a surprise package.
We ordered most of the appetizers from Pani Puri, Hazari Paneer Tikka , Mushroom  Spinach Shashlik, Pav Bhaji Fondue , Nanza and the mind blowing Papdi Chaat.
They were all extremely delicious with mind blowing presentation. The suggested mocktails - Kala Khatta Mojito and Kokum Margherita with Chilli pearls went really well with the appetizers ordered.They have really worked well on presenting the street food more vulnerably to suit the modern culture, thereby retaining the authentic flavor.
Now it was time to order the main course which was well suggested by our server - Paneer Lazeez, Kurkuri Bhindi ( served here as appetizer, but we wanted with the main course), Dal Makhni, Roomali Rotis and the most innovative Biryani - Mushroom Truffle Biryani. OMG!! the best biryani we must have ever had, A MUST TRY.
We ended up having some space forcefully left to try their BUBBLING KULFI - which was outstanding and a superb innovation.
We were so happy to discover this place and would definitely come back with good food cravings. A MUST TRY vegetarian place.
Thank You to the owners who are thoughtful about the idea of opening such a wonderful place.< /review>

GREAT FOOD, BAD CUSTOMER SERVICE!

There was only 1 person waiting ~10 tables during peak dinner crowd (managing indoor and outdoor dining). Got a table outdoor due to the restaurant limiting its indoor capacity to 25% during Covid.

The waiter tried to turn on the heater in the outdoor seating only after 15minutes of customer arrival. It took an extra 5 minutes to replace the gas cylinder and turn on the heater finally. Got a glass of water after these 20 minutes ( after 2 polite requests, screaming once in these 20 minutes)

Got an indoor seating midway and they provided free dessert worth 16$ to compensate for the initial bad customer service. Hence, I am giving an extra star on the rating.

I would expect a fine dine restaurant, that charges ~80$ for 2 people to atleast turn on the heater a little before dinner time on a cold day to make it comfortable for the customers dining outdoors (specially during Covid times when outdoor dining is more popular) & bring water soon upon customer arrival

1 positive: PAV BHAJI FONDUE is delicious</text>

Booked a reservation on opentable for 8.30 PM and went to this restaurant on Sunday night. After reaching there, was told to hurry up before even asked to be seated as the kitchen/restaurant closes at 9 PM :| They should really not have reservation times available this late if it is not well suited for the restaurant's timeline.
After seating, server didn't show up for 10 mins which caused more delay and when he showed up asked us to order everything at once as the kitchen was closing soon. This ruined our entire enthusiasm as this was suppose to be my "birthday dinner / date night" after almost a year of lockdown.
The food was OKish apart from one of the starters.
Our server seemed extremely disinterested and pulled away plates without even asking if we were done with the dish which had some leftovers.
The only upside was the ambience, which was very beautiful and following Covid protocols.
Overall, what was suppose to be an exciting and relaxed birthday dinner turned out to be a stressed experience.<//Text>

< review>
The food here is amazing , both in taste and in the presentation. The kurkure bhindi is especially highly recommended, as an appetizer. We have also ordered the plain naan, chili cheese naan, chili naan , along with a paneer dish. Everything was superb, really amazing the way they presented everything in an unique way, without sacrificing the taste. And if you have sweet tooth like me, please try the flower pot as dessert. It is an amazing amalgamation of rasamalai, chocolate and pistachio dust.

The price is very reasonable , given the food quality and the location. Highly highly recommended.

P.S. I also came to know that they have branches in calcutta, chennai, Bangalore and some of the Indian cities, so that is also something to look forward when I visit my home country.< /review>

(Translated by Google) In May 2019, we took our puppy to Pets R Us, Palmdale. She was bloated and wore diapers because she was bleeding (not in heat). The vet examined her, touched her abdomen and did not notice anything wrong. She asked for some laboratory tests and prescribed antibiotics and cramberry extract to treat a urinary tract infection. When my puppy finished taking the antibiotics, we took her back to the vet with the same symptoms and re-ordered new laboratory tests and also ordered some X-rays. Since she could not see what was wrong with examining the x-rays, she suggested that they be sent to a specialist. They would call us with the results in two days, because it was an urgent matter. A week later, my husband had to go to the doctor's office and wait over an hour for the specialist's report, which was not yet ready. When she received the report, she was told she had to wait another two days because my dog's doctor was on vacation. My husband had to have another doctor explain the results. Another doctor answered him and told him that the results were not clear, but that my dog ‚Äã‚Äãwas supposed to need surgery, pyometry and splenectomy. Then the assistant gave my husband a detailed expense list of about $ 5,000. My husband told them he was going to talk to me first and left. At no time did anyone tell her that my dog ‚Äã‚Äãcould die because the diagnosis was too serious. I asked the doctor to call me and she called the wrong number. We decided that we needed a second opinion and that's why we discovered it was very urgent. Fortunately, we took our puppy to another vet and the first time the doctor examined her, she realized it was something different. She had to repeat the x-rays because the Pets R Us x-rays were taken from the wrong angle. In the end, my dog ‚Äã‚Äãhad a cyst on the ovary. So the diagnosis of Pet R Us was totally wrong, and if it was correct, my dog ‚Äã‚Äãwould have died because they did not tell us that I needed urgent surgery. We contacted Pet R Us for your negligence and to request a refund (almost $ 1000). At first, we were ignored. I had to call them 3 times, in the third opportunity one lied to nois that the manager, Andrew, did not work anymore. After insisting, a person named Jason called me, just to be rude with me and offered me a refund of the hospital visit of about $ 15. That was an insult. After another email, a manager named David called me to have a meeting at the hospital, but we were out of town and had a phone conversation. He fully supported his staff and denied any misdiagnosis even after I had sent them the other veterinarian's medical records with the correct diagnosis. First, he only offered to reimburse the X-rays because he did not want to lose us as clients. When we declined his offer, he offered half the refund and added that we were doing it for revenge. We told him we were doing this because of his misdiagnosis and useless testing at his facility, and especially because our little dog could have died. (Translated by Google) In May of 2019, we took our dog to the location of Pet R Us, Palmdale. She was swollen and had diapers because she was bleeding (and she was not in heat). The veterinarian examined her, touched her abdomen and did not notice anything wrong. He just ordered some laboratory tests and prescribed antibiotics and cranberry extract to treat her with a urinary tract infection. When my dog ‚Äã‚Äãfinished taking the antibiotics, we took her to the vet again, with the same symptoms. The doctor ordered X-rays and more tests. Since he could not see what was wrong while examining the x-rays, he suggested sending them to his specialist. They were going to call us with the results in a couple of days because it was an urgent matter. A week later, my husband had to go to the office and wait more than an hour to get the specialist's report, which they did not have yet. When he received the report, he was told he had to wait another two days because my dog's doctor was on vacation. My husband had to demand that another doctor explain the results. Another doctor told him that the results showed that supposedly my dog ‚Äã‚Äãneeded surgery, pyometra and splenectomy. Then, the assistant gave my husband a detailed list of charges of approximately $ 5,000. My husband told them he was going to talk to me first and he left. At no time, no one told him that my dog ‚Äã‚Äãcould die because the diagnosis was very serious. I asked the doctor to call me and she called the wrong number. We decided that we needed a second opinion and that's why we found out that it was very urgent. Fortunately, we took our dog to another veterinarian and the first time the doctor examined her, she realized that it was something different. He had to repeat the X-rays because those of Pet R Us were taken from the wrong angle. In the end, my dog ‚Äã‚Äãhad a cyst in the ovary. Therefore, the diagnosis of Pet R Us was totally wrong, and if it had been correct, my dog ‚Äã‚Äãwould have died because they did not tell us that she needed urgent surgery. We contacted Pet R Us for their malpractice and to request a refund (almost $ 1000). At first they ignored us. I had to call them 3 times. The last time they lied to us saying that the person in charge, Andrew, did not work there anymore. After insisting, a person named Jason called me, just to be rude to me and offered me a refund of the office visit of approximately $ 15. That was insulting. After another email, a manager named David, called me to have a meeting in the office, but we were out of town and had a chat over the phone. He fully supported his staff and denied any misdiagnosis, even after I sent them the other veterinarian's medical records with the correct diagnosis. First, he only offered reimbursement for the x-rays because he did not want to lose us as clients. When we declined his offer, he offered us half the refund and added that we did it for revenge. We told him that we were doing this because of his misdiagnosis and the useless tests that he carried out in his facilities, and mainly because our dog could have died. It is a shame that Pet R Us only worry about not losing clients, that they are only diligent in giving huge budgets, but that they are not more empathetic and conscientious with the diagnosis and the way in which they communicate valuable information that can save the life of a pet. WE WILL PRESENT A COMPLAINT BEFORE THE VETERINARY BOARD (VETERINARY MEDICAL BOARD)
